Forward Pass"}]}],"\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-3 x:not-first:mt-6 x:list-disc x:ms-6","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Input Data"}],": The input data is fed into the network through the input layer."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Pass Through Layers"}],": The data passes through the hidden layers where each neuron processes the data using weights and an activation function."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-2","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Output Calculation"}],": The final output is produced in the output layer.
